%_where.1 (Arg_0.2: pred[], Arg_1.2: s32[], Arg_2.1: s32[]) -> s32[] {

  %Arg_1.2 = s32[] parameter(1)
  %Arg_2.1 = s32[] parameter(2)
  ROOT %select_n.2 = s32[] select(%Arg_0.2, %Arg_1.2, %Arg_2.1), metadata={op_name="select_n"}
}

%remainder.2 (Arg_0.3: s32[128], Arg_1.3: s32[]) -> s32[128] {
  %Arg_0.3 = s32[128]{0} parameter(0)
  %Arg_1.3 = s32[] parameter(1)
  %constant.98 = s32[] constant(0)
  %eq.1 = pred[] compare(%Arg_1.3, %constant.98), direction=EQ, metadata={op_name="eq"}
  %constant.97 = s32[] constant(1)
  %jit__where_.1 = s32[] call(%eq.1, %constant.97, %Arg_1.3), to_apply=%_where.1, metadata={op_name="jit(_where)"}
  %rem.2 = s32[128]{0} broadcast(%jit__where_.1), dimensions={}, metadata={op_name="rem"}
  %rem.3 = s32[128]{0} remainder(%Arg_0.3, %rem.2), metadata={op_name="rem"}
